style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item&#160;5.02 Departure of Directors or Principal Officers; Election of Directors; Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On January 15, 2024, Chief Commercial Officer James Wilbur and 10x Genomics, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) entered into a Transition and Separation Agreement (the &#8220;Agreement&#8221;) pursuant to which Dr. Wilbur will depart the Company on February 1, 2024. Dr. Wilbur's departure is not due to any disagreement with the Company&#8217;s management team, operations, financial statements, policies or procedures.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Pursuant to the Agreement, Dr. Wilbur will be awarded a one time severance payment of an amount equal to six months of his base salary and a one time COBRA-related payment of $14,335. Dr. Wilbur will not receive an annual performance bonus for the full year 2023. Such payments and benefits are conditioned upon Dr. Wilbur continuing to comply with certain obligations applicable to him and, upon execution and termination, delivery and non-revocation of a general release of claims.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
